<review>I've been here seemingly millions of times to watch the birds and more. I've photographed Red-Tailed Hawks, Great Egrets, Snowy Egrets (but no Snowy Owls!), even a Black Necked Stilt in recent years! I've even spotted a Long-Billed Curlew in these marshes, but PLEASE: this is a protected wildlife area: NO boats, canoes or the sorts, and no walking through the sandy areas. Stay on established paths and trails!! Also a fabulous place to catch a blazing Golden gate sunset!</review>< pictures>

<Rate>5</Rate>< Text>
Crissy Field is part of an urban national park, which, due to its location and scenic views, is popular with both locals, tourists, and dogs.

Crissy Field reopened in 2001. New and rebuilt sidewalks, boardwalks, and trails connect the field north to Fort Point, the Warming Hut (a cafe), and south to the Crissy Field Center, an environmental education center, and the Marina District. Since that time many buildings were restored and leased out as housing, office space, retail, and recreational facilities. The old temporary wood barracks were demolished and the grass airfield restored. Letterman Army Hospital, a large concrete structure, literally was ground to dust and the concrete recycled. In its place George Lucas relocated Industrial Light & Magic.< /Text>

It was great. I came her for a quick getaway/ camping trip with my family and we all enjoyed it. It's quiet and a great place to just relax. Some tips and some things that you should know before coming here is that
1. There is not really any hiking trails in this campground, this is more to relax than to hike.
2. Some spots will have shade and other will not so I recommend coming early so that you get to choose which spot you want.
3. Bring something for kids to do if you bring them because my younger brother was bored after a while.
Overall though, I definitely recommend coming here if you want to have an enjoyable and relaxing time :)< /Text>

<Text>As young children my parents would take us to Chilao a couple times a year to camp in our little Aristocrat RV. We were friends with the on site ranger and his family. We hiked up to the fire watch tower with the ranger a couple of times. Mostly we played on the great rock formations. I pulled my first tooth out while perched  on a rock ledge with my sister.  We caught tadpoles and watched them turn to frogs and made sure to put them pack near the water. I got bit by a neighboring camper‚Äôs dog.  It was my fault for petting it while it was snapping at flies that were pestering him on a hot day.  This dog was bigger than me. It was a giant Great-Dane that looked like Scooby-doo... His big tooth went right thru my the fleshy part of my hand near my thumb and palm.  Those were the good old days when nobody got excited about kids being kids and there was just so much to do in and around all the huge rock formations and the creek that flowed throughout the campsites. The best memories and it was never too crowded.  It‚Äôs a great place to go with kids. We loved it... all 3 of us kids:< /Text>< UserId.>

<Date>1488359523556<//Date><rating>5</rating>< Review>
I came at a time when the campgrounds were first come first serve. We found an awesome spot and camped for a good 2 nights. There weren't too many local trails available to us at the time and the nearby visitors center was closed but that didn't take away too much from our fun.

One downer is that the light pollution from LA is visible from this campground, especially if you're on the side that faces LA. As a matter of fact, you can see the LA lights from the campgrounds at a certain point of the campsite.

They have a couple sites that are meant for bigger groups that offer an amazing view of the mountains but they do require the full double payment.<//Review>

<Review>This campground is easy to get to from the 2 freeway and has some really nice views. The campsites are nice, with firepits, tables, and trees (good for hammocks!). There are many good hikes nearby. Bring your own firewood and water. The sites fill up fast, and are first come first served (not possible to reserve in advance). Folks can be loud on the weekends and there are often partiers. I prefer the quieter weeknights in spring and fall. Summer can be busy all the time.< /Review><rating>4< /rating></record></dataset><record>

< Text>
3 week update:
Clean gym, staff is professional, and the app makes for a smooth experience. The app tells me how crowded the gym is so i can plan accordingly, and the people are very nice and typically mind their own workouts.
Everyone cleans after themselves and there are always plenty of cleaning supplies to ensure the gym stays that way. The lockers here are better than at other places.                          Surprisingly, the showers are still open (limited-capacity, yet I have seen other gyms keep their showers closed), and the lockers feel like a luxury given the very low membership price.
The touchless membership sign-in is also helpful and offers a smooth experience at the entrance (wouldn't mind if it remained after the pandemic ends).
Worth the price.<//Text>

<rating>4< /rating><review>I really like Planet Fitness. I have the $10 a month package and it's worth every penny. I try to go as early as I can after work and usually I can arrive before the big crowds do. Even when there are big crowds, there are still machines available for you to use and the staff are very friendly and helpful. They keep the facilities clean and looking nice. Lucia, the personal trainer, is knowledgable and friendly. She can help you adjust your work out to fit your body's capabilities and suggest things to challenge yourself. I scheduled an appointment to try the 30-minute Express circuit training with her and she had lots of ideas for how I could make it work for me.

The only drawback for this location is parking. It's located in a strip mall and there are many businesses. The hardest time I had trying to find parking was in the evening around 8:30 p.m. I had to park further over by other businesses but there was plenty of lighting. Usually, I can find a parking within 3 minutes any other time. I highly recommend this location!< /review><Pictures>None</Pictures>< Resp>

< Text>
One of my favorite spots to get pastries or a Cuban sandwich! There is no other place that has pastries that taste this good, while costing so little.

Manmi Bakery has such a large variety of pastries to choose from, all under $2. My current favorite is their strawberry croissant. With fresh strawberries topping a fresh and flaky croissant, there's a surprise these filling at the center waiting to just make your tastebuds explode. Their pineapple cheese danish is delicious, and their cheese rolls are so cheap (less than a dollar) and absolutely addicting. Honestly, go nuts and just try one of everything-- you can't go wrong.<//Text>

I was not one attempting to beat all bills but the commercial credit cards, high interest loans and just bad deals paid unreasonable interest rates on for 3 to 4 years, digging my hole deeper. I can say that Yes, the BK law is still available to help for mistakes made, your life is not over if it was just attempting to do the American thing of make things happen.

Of course I‚Äôm aware I‚Äôm luck in retirement, my big concern to protect my retirements for my wife. But their is still help available.

Oaktree Law is a solid family law firm with the principal of a good service in return for a set reasonable fee. I highly recommend their firm, can speak highly of all the staff, the easy and clear preparation of your problem and the best way to solve it for a long term fix and reset in life.

You are welcome to use my name or anything because I am very happy I was able to make the connection with Oaktree Law.<//Text>

< text>
Took my car in yesterday for an oil change and tire rotation which was done satisfactorily as far as I know.  But I also had it in because my window washer fluid system has a leak in it somewhere.  I was told they couldn't find any leak and that maybe I had just used more fluid than I thought (not) and they had filled the reservoir.  Well, I had filled the reservoir previously and by the next day it was empty, and that was without driving anywhere or using the washer at all.  By the time I got home (23 miles) and then later checked the reservoir, it was empty.  No wet spot under the car so it must have leaked out on the way home.  If they didn't have time to do a thorough check or they didn't want to job they should have just told me and not shined me on.  Just because I'm a woman?????  EDIT - I filled the reservoir with water and found the leak myself when I turned on the washer for the front and then the back windows.  Water GUSHED out under the car at the rear.  They could easily have tested those lines just like I finally did.  And I had never said I thought the leak was in the reservoir, I said in the system. Totally incompetent as far as I'm concerned.  UPDATE:  I had called the day after the service to talk to Alex, the service writer that I had dealt with.  He was off that day, but I talked with Manny about the problem with the washer fluid leak still leaking.  Manny is really excellent at customer service, not only dealing with me, but the two instances I had observed while I was originally waiting for my car.  I really had no intention of going back there, but Manny was so sincere about wanting to make things right that I said "OK" and made an appointment for Monday. Alex called me on Friday, I think it was, and was saying how the tech had come to him and he checked also and blah, blah, blah.  I'm no mechanic, but I really don't see how they could NOT have checked the whole system when they couldn't find a leak in the container.  They never even came and asked if I had noticed any wet spots under the car.  Wouldn't have mattered since this was first noticed during those rains.  But don't forget, Alex ASSUMED that I had used more fluid than I realized due to all the butterflys AFTER the rains and wasn't bright enough to realize it.  Never an apology, never saying he wanted to make it right like Manny did, only excuses.  I was talking with my neighbor about the problem a day or so later and he took a look.  The rear hose for my back window washer fluid had come detached and that was where the leak was.  He put it back together and what do you know - no more leak.  Even if the hose wasn't completely apart when in the shop, it HAD to have been loose in order for the container to leak out in a day or day and a half.  Needless to say I will NEVER, EVER go back there again.  And I hope that Alex is given a class in customer service.  ANOTHER EDIT:  Today the owner, Mr. Grady, and I had a conversation and he sincerely apologized for the experience I had.  He even offered a free oil change, which I declined because I'm not out to get any freebies.  I really appreciate his calling me and discussing the situation and for his apology.  Just wanted to let everyone know that he was truly concerned.  However, I still won't go back there.  5/31/19  ADDITIONAL INFO:  When getting the receipt for the oil change, there were several recommendations, one of which was to remove and replace the transmission oil cooler pipes - 3 lines with fittings with 3 quarts of ATF for an estimated $672.  Today I had that work done at another AAA recommended shop which I've used many times before (it's just further away) and it cost $155.00 after my AAA 10 discount.  BIG DIFFERENCE.  I recommend shopping around before using Redhawk Auto.</text>
